FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreateDate], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [b].[Id] AS [Id0], [b].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [b].[Image], [b].[Name] AS [Name0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate1], [c].[Image] AS [Image0], [c].[Name] AS [Name1]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ColorId], [p0].[CreateDate], [p0].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c0] ON [p0].[ColorId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[CreateDate], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[TagId], [t2].[Id] AS [Id0], [t2].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [t2].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [p1].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p2] ON [t].[Id] = [p2].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t1].[Id], [t1].[Id0]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreateDate], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [b].[Id] AS [Id0], [b].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [b].[Image], [b].[Name] AS [Name0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate1], [c].[Image] AS [Image0], [c].[Name] AS [Name1]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ColorId], [p0].[CreateDate], [p0].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [c0].[Name]

) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (

) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p2] ON [t].[Id] = [p2].[ProductId]

SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[BrandId], [t].[CategoryId], [t].[CreateDate], [t].[Description], [t].[Name], [t].[Price], [t].[Id0], [t].[CreateDate0], [t].[Image], [t].[Name0], [t].[Id1], [t].[CreateDate1], [t].[Image0], [t].[Name1], [t0].[Id], [t0].[ColorId], [t0].[CreateDate], [t0].[ProductId], [t0].[Id0], [t0].[CreateDate0], [t0].[Name], [t1].[Id], [t1].[CreateDate], [t1].[ProductId], [t1].[TagId], [t1].[Id0], [t1].[CreateDate0], [t1].[Name], [p2].[Id], [p2].[CreateDate], [p2].[Image], [p2].[IsHover], [p2].[IsMain], [p2].[ProductId]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreateDate], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [b].[Id] AS [Id0], [b].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [b].[Image], [b].[Name] AS [Name0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate1], [c].[Image] AS [Image0], [c].[Name] AS [Name1]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ColorId], [p0].[CreateDate], [p0].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c0] ON [p0].[ColorId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[CreateDate], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[TagId], [t2].[Id] AS [Id0], [t2].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [t2].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [p1].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p2] ON [t].[Id] = [p2].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t1].[Id], [t1].[Id0]

    SELECT TOP(1) [p].[Id], [p].[BrandId], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[CreateDate], [p].[Description], [p].[Name], [p].[Price], [b].[Id] AS [Id0], [b].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [b].[Image], [b].[Name] AS [Name0], [c].[Id] AS [Id1], [c].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate1], [c].[Image] AS [Image0], [c].[Name] AS [Name1]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    INNER JOIN [Brands] AS [b] ON [p].[BrandId] = [b].[Id]
    INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [p].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
    WHERE [p].[Id] = @__id_0
) AS [t]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ColorId], [p0].[CreateDate], [p0].[ProductId], [c0].[Id] AS [Id0], [c0].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [c0].[Name]
    FROM [ProductColors] AS [p0]
    INNER JOIN [Colors] AS [c0] ON [p0].[ColorId] = [c0].[Id]
) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT [p1].[Id], [p1].[CreateDate], [p1].[ProductId], [p1].[TagId], [t2].[Id] AS [Id0], [t2].[CreateDate] AS [CreateDate0], [t2].[Name]
    FROM [ProductTags] AS [p1]
    INNER JOIN [Tags] AS [t2] ON [p1].[TagId] = [t2].[Id]
) AS [t1] ON [t].[Id] = [t1].[ProductId]
LEFT JOIN [ProductImages] AS [p2] ON [t].[Id] = [p2].[ProductId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t].[Id1], [t0].[Id], [t0].[Id0], [t1].[Id], [t1].[Id0]
